msg:This is one of the most beautiful properties I‚Äôve stayed in in Sanya. Gorgeous, tropical, palm filled walkways, palapa gazebos and bridges that span koi filled rivers and ponds ‚Ä¶ I honestly felt I had been transported to Bali. The property is humongous and consists of an impressive lobby of dark wood, and many private villas all decorated in South East Asian decor. My massive room with its impressive view of the jungle below, was at the back of the property (reachable by walking or shuttle cart), on the 6th floor of one of the two tall buildings. It was lovely to soak at night in the December air in the private balcony tub and then crawl into the very comfortable queen bed with its nice linens and feather pillows. Another great feature of this room is that it had a small kitchenette with a full sized fridge and freezer and separate sink. This came in really handy as most restaurants (there is one on the property) were about a 10-15 minute walk away and I  spent most of the time at the property near the pool having stayed at the beach a few days prior to this. The pool itself is also gorgeous, well maintained and equipped with very comfortable loungers situated under shaded palapas among palm trees.The only downside of this hotel I would say is a not-so-nice smell of sulphur (?) that comes and goes depending on where you are on the property. While I don‚Äôt think it would prevent me from coming again, it‚Äôs definitely something to be aware of if you‚Äôre scent sensitive. Thank you to the friendly helpful staff at the front desk for an enjoyable stay at Stony Brook!

posted:Posted August 20, 2021
msg:Fantastic place, we loved it!
Located not too far from Yalong bay beach (about 15 min walk), close to the shopping malls, and the best food market! Plus very reasonably priced compared to other hotels in the area. The territory is huge and green, the service is outstanding, we never waited a minute for the electric car to take us to our building. Overall the personnel was always friendly and eager to help (despite the fact that nobody there could speak English). The room was very spacious with a super comfy bed, great shower and a balcony with an amazing view on the green territory and Yalong bay. There was a bathtub on the balcony which we never even used because the pool was so great (and almost always empty), so we ended up soaking there both day and night (it is open till 11 pm) only going to the beach in the afternoon (the waves were too big anyway). Water bottles refilled daily, the room service was also very good. Breakfast was a very good choice of Chinese food and the common European options (toasts, pastry, cereal, coffee, salad bar). However, then it was changed a bit: salad/fruit bar, pastry and cereal were still there but the rest we had to order from the menu. Anyway it was enough! We also rented a car in Sanya and we were able to park it there in the hotel with no extra charge. The only thing was the WIFI, quite slow and not always I could connect. But the rest was outstanding. Would love to come back there again! Thank you!

the rooms are spacious,beautiful bath and comfortable beds. the air conditioner and fans work well after some time (the rooms are large and need time to cool off)

the pool is much bigger than expected, with a small covered lapa.

the water was clean and warm.

there isn't a convenience store on site but delivery was fine, you just have to collect it at one of the gates or at reception.

there is a bus to the beach from the lobby every half hour but it's only about a 10min walk away.

the beach has a number of seafood restaurants and a burger King and Starbucks. the beach looked nice but it was raining when we were there so can't comment really.

the staff were patient and efficient.

wonderful stay and would stay again despite the relatively long  walk to the beach.

Hotel services are average, non-luxury hotel services. There is only one restaurant, and the breakfast buffet is good, with many choices, but the restaurant closes early, and if you miss a meal, it will close later. There is a canteen next to the restaurant. The free coconut chicken hot pot must be ordered in advance, not on the same day.
You can order takeaway, but it can only be delivered to the hotel service point, and you need to walk or take an electric car to pick up the meal yourself. There is a transfer to the beach, and it takes only 10 minutes to walk to Yalong Bay Beach (public beach).
There is a spy service, but only two people are doing it, and only one person calls and is told that the other one does not know when to come back. It feels like an individual outsourcing service.
Generally speaking, the environment is very good, the room is large, the equipment is relatively old but it doesn't affect it, and the service can't keep up.
5 points for 3.8 points.
